if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != 'fd80c904b53c5a538473f873f6ca8534cd6df060') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fd80c904b53c5a538473f873f6ca8534cd6df060') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '7ab730aa920e0b2b7e73ec95c1826eb311a152e1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fd80c904b53c5a538473f873f6ca8534cd6df060') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'ab6947edca8eba33260c79a4e501dfc239575d0c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'ab6947edca8eba33260c79a4e501dfc239575d0c') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'e377863de8a285ce873f524f1c6a4c2bd3b548fc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'ab6947edca8eba33260c79a4e501dfc239575d0c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') != '70e4ceff72b4fe8288aa94c01205e60257d12783') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '70e4ceff72b4fe8288aa94c01205e60257d12783') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '932bb68690a83e2ba73285eaa3ef4750c8be257f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '70e4ceff72b4fe8288aa94c01205e60257d12783') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') != '630f4855187fee6caa5b4ed9aadd2b9b89dc2a1a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== '630f4855187fee6caa5b4ed9aadd2b9b89dc2a1a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== 'de67d176dd659873601ee1b417752bc19a7fe6b4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== '630f4855187fee6caa5b4ed9aadd2b9b89dc2a1a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php') != '8fd8fd79b1126bb2fd3c80700bf7375ab9962a02') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php') !== '8fd8fd79b1126bb2fd3c80700bf7375ab9962a02') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/java/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php') != '3f73f3e5cce364669ff8f89a2cffd2225dafcba3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php') !== '3f73f3e5cce364669ff8f89a2cffd2225dafcba3') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php') !== '320a78dc75bdf11c5b9e438489a79be512dcb40f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php') !== '3f73f3e5cce364669ff8f89a2cffd2225dafcba3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_29();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php') != '4d04adfea4609858de909d5dfac001a3821dd3c9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php') !== '4d04adfea4609858de909d5dfac001a3821dd3c9') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php') !== 'e7a19ea51bf826248ce822ce6486f43c2810a4ae') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_29();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php') !== '4d04adfea4609858de909d5dfac001a3821dd3c9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/raPages/092_invite/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_33();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/092_invite/plugin.inc.php') !== 'dcab71a136374e14406706023a361da847807abe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/092_invite/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('sitemap.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: sitemap.php');
	writefile_35();
	if (!is_file('sitemap.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): sitemap.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('sitemap.php') != '962c3cb8b7ebe9465028daf3e9d1f0bdab0a4819') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): sitemap.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('sitemap.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of sitemap.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('sitemap.php') !== '962c3cb8b7ebe9465028daf3e9d1f0bdab0a4819') {
		if (@sha1_file('sitemap.php') !== 'c65ef24305ced85aa2f0e13cc6429366669c747b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: sitemap.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('sitemap.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('sitemap.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('sitemap.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_35();
		if (@sha1_file('sitemap.php') !== '962c3cb8b7ebe9465028daf3e9d1f0bdab0a4819') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): sitemap.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php') != 'a57377158f62d270077c38684b81ed7fa9ec7bc3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== 'a57377158f62d270077c38684b81ed7fa9ec7bc3') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/includes/phpsvnclient.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
